The basement is a bit old and it is not easy to park casually. The hotel room is quite clean, but there is a slight smell because the upper floors are not well ventilated. Everyone needs to have windows and doors to create cross ventilation. The sheets and towels are relatively new. The facilities in the bathroom are relatively old. The toilet is an old-fashioned model, and the shower and The bathtub is separated and the floor trea**ent is relatively clean. The light transmittance under the door is relatively bright in the middle of the night. Someone's voice in the corridor can be heard through the room. The sound insulation effect between rooms is still good; the sound when the air conditioner is turned on is old-fashioned. Relatively noisy; the mattress is very soft and may cause back pain while sleeping. Breakfast is located next to the elevator on the first floor of the hotel. It has a lot of breakfast options and is similar to that of a five-star hotel. The buffet in the evening is the highlight. The price is cheap and the ingredients are very fresh. There are many kinds of seafood. The quality of the hot pot shabu-shabu meat is good. Although it is shoddy and shoddy, this dinner buffet is very cost-effective and worth recommending. The surrounding scenic spots are not far away, just a few kilometers away. The location of the hotel is quite convenient. The best experience is the aunties who clean the room. They are very warm, thoughtful and responsive. They are worthy of praise. I will continue to stay here next year. I hope the hotel can go further in terms of hardware and software.
